DANG DNGOS PO DANG, ,MTHONG BA DANG NI SBYIN PA PO, ,'CHING DANG
MCHOG TU ZHI BA DANG, ,THAR DANG DGE BA, THE TSOM DANG, ,GNAS
LA'O NU NI, RJES KHRID DON, ,GNAS DANG RIGS DANG 'DRA BA DANG,,

RGYU YI DON LA BLTA BAR BYA, ,AA PA NAG PO BRAL DON DANG, ,BOR
BA'I DON DANG KLOG PA DANG, ,BRAL DANG MI SDUG CHOM RKUN DGA',
,NGES PAR BSTAN PA DAG LA'O, ,AA BI SRID PA, DGOS PA DANG, ,DRI
DANG, SMOD DANG KUN SDUD DANG, ,RIGS PA TSIG DON

'DOD SPYOD DANG, ,BYA BAR NAMS LA'O AU PA NI, ,DMAN DANG NGAN
DANG KHYAB PA DANG, ,RTZOM DANG, MCHOD PA DAG DANG NI, ,SPYOD MED
BYED PA SBYIN PA DANG, ,SBYIN GNAS DANG NI 'DAS PA DANG, ,AUD NI
BRTZON PA SKYON DANG GTAM, ,'CHI MED DON DANG BTZON PA'I DON,,

BSDU BA DANG NI BYUG 'DOD DANG, ,AU BA'I DON SGRA NI RAB TU
GRAGS, ,BA YI SGRA NI DPE LA 'GYUR, ,CHU LHA LA YANG 'DI NYID DO,
,B'A NI RNAM RTOG DPE DANG NI, ,KHO NA'I DON DANG KUN SDUD PA'O,
,BEE NI RKANG PA KHA SKONG DANG, ,'BREL PA RJES 'KHRID NGES PA'O,
,AA BHI

'DI LTAR GYUR DANG GTAM, ,MNGON PAR 'DOD DANG MNGON DU PHYOGS,
,AA BH'I KshNAm YANG YANG, MYUR, ,PHUL BYUNG DANG NI RGYUD LA'O,
,A'A BHI KAshYAm YANG DE BZHIN TE, ,YANG YANG DANG NI RGYUD LA
'DOD, ,AA M'A LHAN CIG DON DANG, NYE, ,GNAM STONG DANG NI LHAN
CIG GO, ,

@240B AA PA SHYAm NI 'BAD DANG, RTAG ,AA LAm RGYAN DANG, CHOG
TSIG DANG, ,'BRAS MED NUS LDAN THOB DMIGS 'DZIN, ,AI D'A N'I NI,
TSIG RGYAN LA, ,SAm NI SNGAR DON LA YANG 'DOD, ,AI NI SDUG BSNGAL
SGOM PA DANG, ,KHRO DANG MNGON SUM KUN TU 'DZIN, ,AUm NI DRI DANG
KHAB LEN KHRO, ,AUm NI

DRI DANG KHAB LEN KHRO DANG SPYOD, ,AE WAm RNAM PA DPE DANG NI,
,KHAS LEN DANG NI NGES GZUNG DANG, ,AOm NI RJES SU 'DOD PA DANG,
,BRJOD DANG RAB BSNGAGS RIM PA LA, ,KAm NI MGO DANG BDE DANG CHU,
,KA THI DRI BA RNAM PA LA, ,PAm NI G-YO DANG 'BYUNG BA LA, ,MA
MAm RJES

SU 'DOD PA LA, ,PRA NA 'DOD DANG RJES BGROD NYI, ,KAm NI DRI DANG
SMAD PA LA, ,DZO shA TSI SMRA BDE BA DANG, ,RAB TU BSTOD DANG
G-YO BA LA, ,AUDDI NAm NI NYIN CHUD DANG, ,NYI MA SO SOR GNAS PA
LA, ,TUshn'I K'A NI MAm SMA TZAM, ,T'Ushn'I KAm NI THUB PA CAN,
,N'A MA RAB GSAL

'BYUNG BA DANG, ,NGAN DANG KHAS LEN KHRO BA LA, ,NU NAM RNAM PAR
RTOG PA DANG, ,DON NGES PA LA RNAM PAR BSHAD, ,PR'A DHV'A GUG PA
RJES SU MTHUN, ,PHUL BYUNG NGES DANG SHIN TU'I DON, ,SHAm NI DGE
DANG BDE BA LA, ,SAm NI CHAGS DON MNYAM PA'I DON, ,MDZES

PA'I DON DANG PHUL BYUNG DON, ,SMA NI 'DAS DANG RKANG PA SKONG,
,SA M'A SMOD DANG GNYIS LDAN LA, ,SAm PRA TAm NI DA LTAR BA, ,HAm
NI KHRO TSIG RJES KHRID LUS, ,PRA GU NGA NI RNAM RTOG LA, ,H'U NI
RNAM GNON RJES SU 'DOD, ,SDIG PA LA YANG 'GA' ZHIG 'DOD, ,AA YI
K'A

NI CHA, SHAS NGAN, ,SMRA BA RTOGS DANG DGA' TSIG DANG, ,G-YUL
NGOR SON DANG RJES KHRID DANG, ,'GRO DANG KUN 'KHOR KHRO BA LA,
,A'A YA DRAN DANG DUG SOGS DANG, ,DUS MTHA' DANG NI DBUS DAG LA,
,AANTA R'A NI BRAL DON DANG, ,DBUS KYI DON DANG NYE BA'I DON,,

AANTAR RAB MTHA'I DON DBUS DON, ,RANG GI BYED DON RNAMS LA BLTA,
,AU RA R'I DANG A'U RA R'I, ,A'U R'I, RGYA CHE RANG GIR BYAS,
,DUR NI DGAG PA, DKA' TSEGS DANG, ,'GRO SOGS DON DANG PHUL BYUNG
MIN, ,NIR NI MA LUS DGAG PA DANG, ,BHRi SHA SOGS DON NGES

@241A *, ,PA LA, ,PA R'A RTOGS PA GNOD PA DANG, ,SO SOR SMRA DANG
GTZO BO MCHOG ,MNGON PHYOGS RNAM PAR THAR PA DANG, ,NGES PA'I DON
DANG RNAM GNON LA, ,PA RI KUN NAS DNGOS PO DANG, ,THOB 'DOD MTSAN
NYID LA SOGS DANG, ,'KHYUD

DANG GOS DANG KHYAB PA DANG, ,NAD DANG MYA NGAN MCHOD PA MCHOG
,SA SKYONG SKYON BSHAD BOR BA LA, ,PHU NAR DBYE BA DANG PO DANG,
,SNGA MAR GYUR PA SNGON RABS DANG, ,RAB BCINGS NYID DANG 'DAS PA
DANG, ,SA BLA MTHO RIS 'JIG RTEN GZHAN, ,KE LA MDZES DANG

LO RGYUS DANG, ,SRID PA DANG NI RJES KHRID DON, ,KHA LU TSIG
RGYAN THOB 'DOD DGAG ,NGES DANG RGYUN DANG MI SMRA DANG, ,SHES
'DOD LA SOGS RNAMS LA DRAN, ,AA BA KHYAB DANG YONGS BSGOM DANG,
,BRAL PA DMIGS PA DGAG PA DANG, ,CHUD ZAD DON DANG RNAM

SHES DANG, ,DPE DANG NGES PAR GZUNG BA LA, ,BAS NI KHYED RNAMS
SHES DON DANG, ,DBYE BA DANG NI RNAM PA DANG, ,'DAS DANG THA DAD
DON GTZO DANG, ,DNGOS PO DANG NI MKHA' 'GO LA'O, ,AU sh'A GRANGS
DANG, GRANGS BCAS DANG, ,MTSAN MO'I MTHA' DANG NGES

NYAL 'DOD, ,DO sh'A, MTSAN MO'I SGO DANG NI, ,MTSAN MO DANG NI
SPRIN LA YANG, ,MI shA sh'A NI MTHA' DANG DBUS, ,BSRUNG BA DANG
NI GZHAN LA YANG, ,AA GRA TAS NI DANG PO DANG, ,RTZE MO MCHOG
DANG DE NYID DANG, ,MI SMRA RNAMS SO, AA BHI TA, ,MTHA' DANG

MTHA' DAG MNGON PHYOGS DANG, ,GNYI GA DANG NI MYUR BA LA, ,TI RAS
BDUD 'GRO MI SNANG DANG, ,NGAL BA DANG NI DGAG PA DANG, ,MTHA'
DAG PA DANG NI 'DAS PA DAG ,N'I TZI RANG DBANG CHUNG BAR 'DOD,
,PU RAS MCHOG DANG DANG PO LA, ,BU RANG SA NA DANG PO

MCHOG ,PRA TAS SNGA NYIN SNGA DRO LA, ,PURBED++YUS NI CHOS KYI
GNAS, ,SNGA MA'I DON DANG KHA NYIN DANG, ,PHYI PHYIR DANG NI YANG
DANG YANG, ,MANG BA'I DON LA MI THA STE, ,PHAN TSUN DANG NI
'PHROG PA'O, ,PR'A DUS RAB GSAL SPYOD PA DANG, ,SRID PA TZAM
LA'ANG BLTA BA'O, ,

@241B SA NEES, DAL BUS RGYU BAR BSHAD, ,RANG DBANG DANG NI LEGS
MCHOD DANG, ,NGES PA'I DON DANG RJES SU BGROD, ,DKA' TSEGS DANG
NI YANG DAG 'BYOR, ,DE DUS TZAM DANG BAB CHOL DANG, ,GLO BUR
BYUNG BA LA YANG NGO, ,MA H'A MYA NGAN LAS SKYES DANG, ,NGAN

DANG DUG DANG SNYING RJE'I DON, ,AA HO, 'DRI DANG RNAM DPYOD
DANG, ,RMAD BYUNG SKYONG BA RNAMS LA 'DOD, ,AA H'A H'A NI NGO
MTSAR SKYE, ,AA HA HA NI PHRA RGYAS DANG, ,YONGS SU NYON MONGS
RAB DGA' LA, ,A'A HA, SKYONG DANG NGES SBYOR DON, ,AU T'A HO NI
'DI DAG

RTOG; ,SA HA'I SGRA NI MTHA' DAG DANG, ,CIG CAR DANG NI YANG DAG
SBYOR, ,'DRA DANG YOD DANG 'BREL PA LA, ,HA NI RKANG PA KHA SKONG
DANG, ,'BREL PA DANG NI DMAN PA'O, ,H'A NI DUG LA SOGS PA LA,
,H'A H'A SKYO BA LA RAB GRAGS, ,DRI ZA LA YANG, ,H'A H'A'O, HE NI

BYE BRAG NGES GZUNG DANG, ,RKANG PA KHA SKONG DAG LA'O, ,H'I NI
NGO MTSAR DUG SOGS DANG, ,DGA' DANG SDUG BSNGAL RGYU RNAMS LA'O,
,H'I H'I NGO MTSAR DGOD PA LA, ,H'U H'A DGA' DANG DRI ZA LA, ,HA
HEE YONG MIN DRAN PA DANG, ,BOD PA DANG NI RGYU RNAMS LA, ,HO
DANG

HO NI MTHA' DAG DANG, ,BOD PA DANG NI 'GRAN PAR 'DOD, ,MI KshVA,
MYUR DANG NGES PA'I DON, ,DE NYID LA YANG 'GA' ZHIG 'DOD, ,MI ZAD
PA DON DU MA CAN RNAMS SO, ,BAL PO'I LO SUM BRGYA BRGYAD CU RTZA
GCIG PA LAS, DBO'I ZLA BA'I NAG PA'I TSES BRGYAD GZA'

PHUR BU'I NYIN, DPAL ROL PA'I GRONG, GOO TA MA LHAG PAR GNAS PA'I
GTZUG LAG KHANG CHEN POR, PAndI TA GNAS BRTAN DPAL RIGS MCHOG
DPAL YE SHES KYIS 'DRIR BCUG PA'I SDE TSAN RDZOGS SO,, ,,'DI NI
LHA DANG MI YI YON

GYI SPYAN SNGA RIN PO CHE'I ZHAL SNGA NAS KYI BKA' BZHIN, ZHA LU

'GYUR GYI 'CHI
